Its patented SmoothSip spout is ergonomically shaped to fit your mouth, so every sip feels, well… smooth. Paired with a sliding lock lid that clicks firmly shut, you can toss it in your bag without stressing over spills. There’s also a sturdy, easy-to-carry handle that makes it simple to grab and go—whether you’re commuting, running errands, or just walking from the kitchen to your desk. The 12oz size is perfect for your daily caffeine fix, and the tapered base fits most car cupholders for commute-friendly sipping. Thanks to the triple-layered vacuum insulation, your drink stays hotter and colder for longer. The wide-mouth opening makes it easy to drop in ice or give it a quick clean, while the durable stainless steel build is tough enough for everyday use. And it's safe as can be, thanks to its BPA, lead, and phthalate-free materials. Long story short, SmoothSip Slider with Handle is the handy (pun intended) sidekick your coffee's been waiting for. Its patented SmoothSip spout is ergonomically shaped to fit your mouth, so every sip feels, well… smooth. Paired with a sliding lock lid that clicks firmly shut, you can toss it in your bag without stressing over spills. There’s also a sturdy, easy-to-carry handle that makes it simple to grab and go—whether you’re commuting, running errands, or just walking from the kitchen to your desk. The 24oz size is perfect for your daily caffeine fix, and the tapered base fits most car cupholders for commute-friendly sipping. Thanks to the triple-layered vacuum insulation, your drink stays hotter and colder for longer. The wide-mouth opening makes it easy to drop in ice or give it a quick clean, while the durable stainless steel build is tough enough for everyday use. In addition to our patented 2-in-1 FreeSip spout (you know, the one with the built-in straw and open swig option), this 40oz stainless steel water bottle holds plenty of water without being oversized. The sturdy bucket handle makes it easy to grab and go—not to mention comfy to hold. The tapered shape fits pretty much anywhere you’d stash a bottle, including most cupholders—whether it’s your car or your spin bike. The triple-layer insulation keeps drinks cold for up to 24 hours, and the sweat-proof exterior means no slippery hands or water rings.The wide-mouth opening makes cleaning easy and adding ice even easier. Plus, it’s made with BPA-free, durable materials. Sway is the ultimate hydration companion that goes with the flow of your day. It’s the ultimate gift for anyone who needs to up their hydration game. In addition to our patented 2-in-1 FreeSip spout (you know, the one with the built-in straw and open swig option), this 30oz stainless steel water bottle holds plenty of water without being oversized. The sturdy bucket handle makes it easy to grab and go—not to mention comfy to hold. The tapered shape fits pretty much anywhere you’d stash a bottle, including most cupholders—whether it’s your car or your spin bike. The triple-layer insulation keeps drinks cold for up to 24 hours, and the sweat-proof exterior means no slippery hands or water rings.The wide-mouth opening makes cleaning easy and adding ice even easier. Plus, it’s made with BPA-free, durable materials. Sway is the ultimate hydration companion that goes with the flow of your day. It’s the ultimate gift for anyone who needs to up their hydration game. In addition to our patented 2-in-1 FreeSip spout (you know, the one with the built-in straw and open swig option), this 30oz stainless steel water bottle holds plenty of water without being oversized. The sturdy bucket handle makes it easy to grab and go—not to mention comfy to hold. The tapered shape fits pretty much anywhere you’d stash a bottle, including most cupholders—whether it’s your car or your spin bike. The triple-layer insulation keeps drinks cold for up to 24 hours, and the sweat-proof exterior means no slippery hands or water rings.The wide-mouth opening makes cleaning easy and adding ice even easier. Plus, it’s made with BPA-free, durable materials. Sway is the ultimate hydration companion that goes with the flow of your day. It’s the ultimate gift for anyone who needs to up their hydration game. The versatile 2-in-1 FreeSip spout lets you drink upright through a built-in straw or tilt back for a regular swig. Built for comfort, convenience, and clean sipping : Hygienic push-button lid keeps spout clean; double threaded lid and side handle are right-handed and left-handed friendly The double-wall insulation keeps drinks cold for up to 24 hours, and the wide opening makes it easy to add ice and clean. The base fits most cup holders. Made from safe, BPA, lead, and phthalate-free materials. The lid is dishwasher safe, but the cup should be hand washed. Not for use with hot liquids. Description Get a handle on your hydration with the Owala FreeSip® Tumbler. This 40oz water bottle is designed to keep up with your daily routine—whether you’re commuting to work, running errands, or just trying to drink more water. The standout feature? Our patented FreeSip® spout. It’s a 2-in-1 design that gives you options: sip through the built-in straw or tilt it back for a big swig. The choice is yours. With 40 ounces to work with, that’s enough water to last you through meetings, workouts, or a full day pickleball tournament. Plus, its triple-layer insulation keeps drinks cold for up to 24 hours without breaking a sweat. Always on the move? This lockable lid will lock down your liquids. The built-in handle is sturdy, comfy, and made for righties and lefties. The wide mouth opening makes cleaning and adding ice easy. Plus, this water bottle is BPA free, leak resistant, and contoured to fit in cup holders. Basically, it checks all the boxes—and makes the ultimate gift for water-loving humans. With a built-in, easy-clean straw and a wide-mouth opening, the FreeSip reusable bottle is designed for drinking two different ways: sipping upright through the straw or tilting back to swig from the wide-mouth spout opening. Add in a push-to-open lid and playful colors, and staying hydrated has never been simpler—or more fun. Additional features include double-wall insulated stainless steel that keeps drinks cold up to 24 hours, a carry loop that doubles as a lock, a cup holder-friendly base, and a wide opening for easy cleaning and adding ice. The Owala FreeSip Insulated Stainless-Steel Water Bottle with Locking Push-Button Lid is available in three sizes: 24-Ounce, 32-Ounce, and 40-Ounce. Lid is dishwasher safe; hand wash cup. Not for use with hot liquids. Manufacturer’s limited lifetime warranty. With a built-in, easy-clean straw and a wide-mouth opening, the FreeSip reusable bottle is designed for drinking two different ways: sipping upright through the straw or tilting back to swig from the wide-mouth spout opening. Additional features include double-wall insulated stainless steel that keeps drinks cold up to 24 hours, a carry loop that doubles as a lock, a cup holder-friendly base, and a wide opening for easy cleaning and adding ice. The Owala FreeSip Insulated Stainless-Steel Water Bottle with Locking Push-Button Lid is available in five colors. Lid is dishwasher safe; hand wash cup. Not for use with hot liquids. With a built-in, easy-clean straw and a wide-mouth opening, the FreeSip reusable bottle is designed for drinking two different ways: sipping upright through the straw or tilting back to swig from the wide-mouth spout opening. Add in a push-to-open lid and Harry Potter house colors, and staying hydrated has never been simpler—or more fun. Additional features include double-wall insulated stainless steel that keeps drinks cold up to 24 hours, a carry loop that doubles as a lock, a cup holder-friendly base, and a wide opening for easy cleaning and adding ice. The Owala FreeSip Insulated Stainless-Steel Water Bottle with Locking Push-Button Lid is available in four house colors, just ask the Sorting Hat: Gryffindor, Slytherin, Ravenclaw, and Hufflepuff. Lid is dishwasher safe; hand wash cup. Not for use with hot liquids. Manufacturer’s limited lifetime warranty.
